et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and the pain jumps out, as we have said regarding the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this procedure, there is danger that the patient dies immediately, or a fistula develops that cannot be healed.
de la mice	about the spleen
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the spleen with what we have discussed in the sections on treatments, and it is not effective, then there are three types of cautery that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	One of these methods is to make three or four cauteries, in a line along the length of the spleen, similar to the shape of the cautery for the liver that we discussed before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand hard during the cauterization, and have the patient lie on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	And another method of cauterization is to heat the cautery that has two prongs, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the skin that is next to the spleen, where the patient's ribs are on the left side, and the elevation with which you lift the skin should be lengthwise along the body, and the cauteries should be across the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Afterward, insert the two heated prongs until the skin is pierced on the other side, and then pull out the cautery, and thus there will be four (marks).
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, cauterize with the three-pronged cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	Treat it afterward when it has discharged pus for a long time, and this is better than the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not useful for dropsy, except in the manner called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in the sections, and your treatment is not effective, then you must make four cauteries around the groin, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one near the chest;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cautery be very close to the thickness of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open to drain pus for a long time, and do not abandon the care of the patient after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will be hastened, and the two intentions will be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly should be the key (cautery iron) that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what is placed above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who has dropsy, and are full of citrine-colored water, you must cauterize on the top of the foot between the little toe and the ring toe;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery without twisting.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go in too deeply, thus the citrine water will come out, and the cautery should be according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Afterwards, make two cauteries on the legs, one on each leg at the tip of the calf muscle;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and the cautery should be long, one below the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries open for a long time without cleaning, so that the water comes out;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	afterwards treat with the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the lessening/reduction
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When diarrhea comes from cold and moisture, so much so that the retentive and digestive power which is in the stomach and intestines is weakened, and cannot be treated by ways of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and with strong constitution, then make a large cautery on the stomach according to what has been discussed previously regarding cautery of the stomach, with the circular cautery;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four cauteries around the navel, small, with a small key-shaped cautery, and two cauteries on the hips. 
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, then make a cautery on the spine, and a cautery on each flank, and two small cauteries on the stomach next to the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance/constitution.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are in the anus, one or more, and are old and consist of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as we have described in divisions/sections, and it is not effective, then make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the spine, the one that is furthest outside, beneath the shoulder blade little by little in a triangular shape, and one cautery below the navel two fingers;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think that his stomach is chilled, and the food does not digest, and one sees swelling in the face, then make a large cautery on the stomach, as mentioned before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with the key-shaped cautery;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After, treat the area until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshy growth that is called "thelul" (keloid)
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the keloid, heat a cautery that resembles a razor, and then place it, while still burning, on the cut keloid;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and keep your hand there until the cautery reaches the base of the vein from which the blood flows;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is a lot of keloid, cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	afterwards treat them with beneficial ointments until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the keloid, it will have a greater effect.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly healed wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or opening, which we will discuss in its place, such an illness arises that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When someone develops a fistula, and it is aged and releases pus and corrupted fluids, you should probe it completely with a thin tent, and make sure you know with the tent how deep it is.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	Afterward, heat the cautery that resembles a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to the depth that the tent has entered, and repeat the cautery until the rotten and corrupted flesh is burned, once, or twice, or three times, according to the amount needed;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and be careful not to burn the nerves that are there, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and to the intestine, beware of these places, and do not do this except in fleshy areas, and consider that it is not piercing;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	Afterward, treat the area until it is healed, and if the place is sealed, and the infected matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the area is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the infected matter is not removed, know that the place is perforated, and the bone at the bottom is corrupted;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and as with one of those that we will describe in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When kidney pain comes from cold, and from great flatulence, and there is no desire for a woman, then you must make cauteries on the kidneys on one side and the other with the key-shaped cautery that we have mentioned before;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have three cauteries in a line, and they will do more good.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make cauteries on the outside above the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, one on the right and one on the left, and let each cautery be as long as the joint of a thumb;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make one cautery on the lower back outside, or two if you need to;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cautery be key-shaped according to the aforementioned form.
de la marris	of the spleen
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the spleen is cold and moist, and yet does not prevent conception, and the menses are corrupted and their periods delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, she feels great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to make three cauteries around the navel, as we have described in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries outside the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and the cautery should be key-shaped, as we have described.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous humors descend to the hip socket, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when they are measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the place of the separation is found empty, it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the hip socket with a cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the place around the socket as it turns, so that the socket is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and the cautery should be like the one used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not available, make three large olive-shaped cauteries, and the cautery should be as deep as the skin;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the socket of the hip, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is treated as we have described in the section and the treatment is ineffective, and the illness is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the patient of the thick humors with foul-smelling pills, or other similarly good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterwards, apply cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of cautery is as follows, in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, with burning medicines together, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is done in many ways, one of which is this:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the point of the hip, three triangular cauteries in this form, and make them good and deep and wide, and have between each cautery a space the width of a finger, and the cautery should be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes one makes a cautery in the middle, on the top of the hip, therefore there are four, in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, cauterize it with the circular cautery that we mentioned before in the dislocation of the hip;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle encompasses the entire hip, and all the thickness of the flesh is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used for sciatica, when the pain is located in the hip, and doesn't reach down to the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the thigh and leg, make two cauteries where the patient says the pain is, and one cautery above the ankle, four fingers up, slightly to the left side; 
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and the cautery should be knife-shaped, and burn through the thickness of the flesh;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels the pain extending to the toes of the foot or nearly so, cauterize where they feel the pain, three or four points with the cautery called "point cautery".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, make more;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it is known that the pain is below the knee toward the thigh, make a cautery with the knife-shaped or circular cautery, and take great care in all your cauteries not to leave the cautery in so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient further harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have made cauteries on the ankle of the foot, and left them in so long that the leg was completely swollen, and the foot as well, and the entire foot was pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bowel movement, from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, make a cautery in one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said regarding the cautery of the hip, of which this is the method: make such an iron and let it be at the tip as thick as the fingernail of a thumb, or a little less, and let it be serrated and let it be from one serration to the other a distance the size of a thumb knuckle;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the serrations be angled on two sides, and let them be like knots, and let there be a well-made iron handle;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is all red and throws off sparks, and then place it on the buttock of the afflicted hip, and turn it onto the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize it once with a round cautery and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make a plaster of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating it with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of fear of its appearance, and we see few who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and yet this is one of the good cauteries, for those who can bear it, and where it is appropriate.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of burning medicine is made with an instrument with openings into which the edge of the opening descends, and it should be of brass or iron with a long side, and at the top it should have two knots, and between each the width of a finger;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they should be open below and above, and joined together in this way:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Then place it on the buttock of the patient lying on his healthy side, and press your hand firmly on the buttock;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	then pour between the two rings hot water that has been heated on the fire for a while, and leave it for an hour, and let the patient endure the heat and the burning from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it finds there a mortification as if by fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the mortification has passed, remove your hand with the instrument and wash the buttock with fresh water, and leave it thus for three days, and apply butter until what is blackened by the burn is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it three days so that the pus comes out;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final treatment after the application of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument that holds water just as you did for the buttock;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method for hot water, and I have written it in the treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal amounts of each, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole below so that the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place another well-sealed pot on top of this pot, and put alkali and lime and fresh water on top, until there is a finger's width above the powders when you have pressed it well with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it like this until sharp water descends and falls into the sealed pot, then take all this water, and throw it onto lime and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very sharp and is administered in many medical procedures and in cauterizations of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it does the same work as fire, and there are other medicines with which one can cauterize the hip well, such as orpiment and anacardic honey and lime with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment with which a man was cured of hip pain and sciatica, and praises it highly, and says that no other treatment was done, and that he was healed in a single instance when this treatment was performed, and he had bathed as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And says in this manner that you take fresh, dry green litharge, and grind it well with a little fat, and put it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and bind it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours, or as long as it takes until the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then have him enter the bath until his body is a little moistened, and have him go to bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use cautery with such medicines, unless it is after the body has been evacuated.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat dung, it helps a lot;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery should be done in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it on the hollow that is between the big toe and the next one, which is called foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Then take dry goat dung and ignite it until it becomes coals, and put it on the wool, and leave it there until it is extinguished;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do it again this way, and do not stop doing so until you think, by reason, that it reaches the hip, and that the pain has ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this type of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or from a blow or by too great an evacuation, or from some sort of spread cold matter, for none of these cases is cautery useful, except for the one that comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient has been purged with foul-smelling pills or other such, that three lines marked with ink be made on his back, there where the pain is located, and on each line five cauteries or more according to the strength and the amount that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cautery should be done according to the cautery which is called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you wish, make three or four cauteries with the medium key cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Often this illness comes to small children, and the sign of the onset is that they have shortness of breath when they rise, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find on the last spinal process of the back and on us the appearance that comes upon the other spinal processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to treat it, cauterize it with the circular cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery affects each part of the spinal process equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish, cauterize around the spinal process with the pointed cautery two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After, treat the area until it is healed according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cautery to a curvature that is in a nerve spasm.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pains are from humors that are spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes in the feet, which doctors properly call "gout," and when it is from a cold cause and treatments with medicines cannot cure it, it is treated by cauteries in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary that you prick on the surface of the foot, make a cautery with the entire cautery that is called "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and to the other joints, and this happens many times, make three or four cauteries on each knee, on each side, with the olive-shaped cautery;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you need more, make more, but do not hold your hand there longer than it takes to burn the thickness of leather.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and to the back, administer the cautery that we have described in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make punctures around the wrist in two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if any pain remains in the fingers, make punctures on each joint and on the back of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains reach the elbows or up to the shoulders, cauterize each part, and ensure the patient has good care and takes medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good care and purge phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the peritoneum
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the groin, and the intestines descend into the scrotum, and this is recent, it is necessary that when you intend to treat it, he does not eat anything that day; 
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things that loosen the bowels, so that the feces descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	afterwards have him sit on his back between your hands, and tell him to hold his breath until the intestines are returned, and put them back with your fingers, and make an incision below the rupture on the pubic bone, and also another incision shaped like half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery, of which this is the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and throws off sparks.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then return the intestines to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the assistant should hold his hand there so they don't return;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open the patient's thighs well, and place a cushion under him and an attendant on his thighs, and another on his chest to hold his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery on the mark with your whole hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, do it again until you reach the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and carefully watch that the intestine does not protrude when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that because of this the patient does not die, or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And the cautery for children must be small according to their size, and for adults as large according to their size;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, treat the site of the cautery with butter until the burn is gone;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	Afterward, treat it with other ointments until it is healed, and the patient should lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well closed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and their food should be cooked for a long time, so that their bowels do not move when they try to go to the toilet.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when they want to get up, apply a well-made support bandage, and wear it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and they should rest well, working little and avoiding overfilling themselves with drink and food, and avoid shouting too loudly;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when they follow these instructions, they will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will discuss the treatment of cutting in its own chapter below.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other abdomens and are recognizable, and you see that they are not growing, then make a round cautery according to its size, and burn a third of the core;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	afterwards treat it according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a three-angled cautery in this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the location with ink and draw a line across the width above the rupture, and another outside it, and hold your hand in the middle with the cautery firmly in place.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cautery is easier and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in a limb, either from a fall or a blow, and this pain lasts a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it must be cauterized with a cautery called "points," and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb and its size and weakness and its strength and its location with regard to twisting and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed from the first cautery, that is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if not, repeat another cautery over that one, for such is the custom that it should move to the nearest limb, therefore you must perform the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of leprosy
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Lepers are sometimes greatly helped by cautery, and especially those illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see it to be cauterized, take care if the illness is at the beginning, and if it is treated according to what we have said in the division, and neither descends nor remains, and you fear that the corruption will take hold of the whole patient, then make five cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	One in the middle of the head to the occiput, and the other towards the forehead at the hairline;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two on the two temples, and one behind on the nape of the neck;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and press your hand so that the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the scabs come out so that the vapors of the thick humors can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize it on the spine according to what is described before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the measles are spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is clearly evident, then you must cauterize it with these cauteries that we have mentioned on the head, and one cautery on the bridge of the nose, and two cauteries on the spine of the neck, and six cauteries on the spine of the back, and one large one on the rump and another next to it, and two on the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the elbows, and two on the tendons of the breast, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on the back heel, that you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes one makes a cautery on the wrist bone, and another on the breastbone, and another on the liver. 
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauteries you make, the more help you give, and the more it benefits him;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the sick person does not feel pain from the cautery as the healthy feel it, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And the cauteries must be large and small according to the limbs and joints, depending on how you find it in the types of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterward, treat the area with vetch flour with honey and other treatments until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then make cauteries on the limb according to the size of the limb;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cautery go a little into the thick part of the flesh;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes one makes a cautery on the hand and on the foot and on the back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and yet no one should undertake this unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	of albaras (white leprosy/vitiligo)
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness called "albaras" is chronic, and medical remedies are of no use, then cauterize it with a shallow cautery, according to the thickness of the skin, until the whiteness is removed and its color is changed;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then treat it with flour of vetches and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and pigeon blood and lark blood, one part of each;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix it all together, and bind it with a cloth, and leave it on the spot until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of chancre by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre appears at the beginning, and you want to stop it, cauterize it with a cautery that resembles a circle, all around the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And yet, wise men say that one should also cauterize in the middle of the chancre;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and yet, this does not seem good to me, for I fear that it will be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have seen it happen sometimes;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and it is more appropriate that it be cauterized around, with the cautery which is called "circular," as we have said about cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling that cannot mature/suppurate/come to a head
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness that is called "adubelati", and it is slow to mature/suppurate/come to a head either because of the excess matter it produces or because of the patient's age when he is decrepit (that is to say, too old) and he has little blood, or because of the weather/season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you want to hasten its maturation/suppuration:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around it with many small cauteries by pricking/puncturing;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards leave it like that.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to mature/suppurate/come to a head.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you want to pierce it completely with the cautery, then heat the cautery which has this shape:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called “adubelati” until the cautery has pierced the core, and let the cautery be such that the patient feels it from the outside in such a way that the flow of pus is facilitated/released. 
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards treat it until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment with fire by iron/cautery
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another type of disease which is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a consumption of the limb, for it consumes the limbs as fire does dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can tolerate cautery with fire, then heat the cauteries, both small and large nails, according to what is suitable for the place where the disease is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	afterwards cauterize it on all sides until you eradicate all the corruption, and none of it remains, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply on the cauterized areas crushed sulfur with oil until the burns from the fire are gone, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterwards treat it with ointments that generate flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy flesh is not growing, it is good; 
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then repeat the cauterization on what remains of the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this affliction was sometimes treated with sharp medicine instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nevertheless fire cautery is of greater benefit, and I have already described the treatment with sharp medicine in the section:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take it when you have need of it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the pores/holes that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Very often it happens that on the outside of the feet a malady arises which is called "nail/corn/boil" according to our understanding, and it is a large, infected thing which hurts the foot. 
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization of this malady is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say cauterization by fire, and cauterization by hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cauterization by fire is that you heat a cautery instrument like the quill of a vulture's feather, and it should be made of good iron in such a way that it can enclose the nail/corn/boil on all sides, and that it has thin edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	afterwards put it, all hot, on the nail/corn/boil, and turn your hand all around the nail/corn/boil until it reaches the bottom of the nail/corn/boil;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it thus for three days until it begins to discharge pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail/corn/boil will fall off and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the area with an ointment that generates flesh until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned outwards from the body, and often occur on the hands and feet, you must apply a hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a chain of brass or iron, or a vulture's feather, and put it on the nail/corn/boil and the wart, that is to say, warts and verrucas;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the chain so that it surrounds everything, then put some hot water in it, and hold your hand firmly, and squeeze your hand while turning so that the edge of the chain reaches the root of the nail/corn/boil, and the hot water can find a deep path to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer the burning of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it like that, and it will uproot itself completely with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this one after the other, until you have removed all those that are on the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment of tremors/shaking/shivering
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone trembles from nerve coldness, or quartan fever or other, you should make four cauteries on the spine of the back, one cautery between each vertebra;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cautery on the feet, and one on the stomach with an olive-shaped cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	this will stop the trembling, and hasten the recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	stinking pustules / of stinking pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes bumps, or stinking pustules, appear on the outer body, which come from large corrupted materials/humors.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	So, first, when they appear, a cautery must be made on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery of myrtle wood, whose tip is set on fire, or of long birthwort root, or with a lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this way, and they cannot grow further from then on, but the superfluity from which they come is broken, and they are healed;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But this must be done after bloodletting.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often there are large flows of blood from the artery that is cut in a wound that occurs superficially, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cauterization of a limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very difficult to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And nevertheless when this happens to someone, quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the blood is calmed under your finger, and no more drops come out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then put several small and large olive-shaped cauteries in the fire until they are all red-hot;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take one, either large or small depending on the wound and the place where the artery is broken, and put the cautery on that vein where you are holding your finger, and hold the cautery there until the blood is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it spurts out when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, quickly take another one of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is stanched;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood flows from the artery, it cannot be easily stopped, especially when the artery is large, except by one of the four methods that we have described:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	either by cautery, or by extraction when it is not cut, or by tight tying with thread, or by medicines applied that have the power to stop blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and it should be tied and tightly bound.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever attempts to stop the bleeding by tightly binding cloths or by putting burning things on it, or other similar things, will achieve little benefit.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to someone and they do not have a doctor or medicine present, they should put their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and press firmly until the bleeding is stopped above the wound and above the vein; 
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not remove the finger, but wet it often with cold water, very cold, until the blood is congealed and thickened and stopped;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and then do what is necessary with cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We told you in the first chapter every illness where cautery by fire, or burning medicine, is necessary, and the occasions and the causes and the instruments and the methods of cauterization;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have arranged this chapter from head to toe, and I will continue in this chapter in the same manner so that one can more easily find what one desires.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And before I begin this, dear son, you must understand that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first one on cauteries, and therefore greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	Thus come some who are so angered by their illness that they die easily because of the fury they find in their sickness, and the greatness of its malice;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and of these one must be wary.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And among these are some who give you their trust and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is deceptive.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not agree with those who come to you with this attitude, but place more value on your honor than on your greed, and do not act foolishly but wisely in what you are certain of, and from which you can gain reward and praise;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indication in the treatment of your patients so that it leads to healing;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire a good reputation, and glory, and the memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and may He inspire you with the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have arranged this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what is before in the chapter on cauteries, which I described to you from head to toe, so that you may more easily find what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	of the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often occurs in children at birth, and when the midwife squeezes the child's head too hard;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from a hidden cause that is unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness except in children, and in all those I have seen, death came quickly;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and therefore it seems to me that it is better to abandon the work in such treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and the head grew every day so much that he could not support it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the fluid grew so much that he died, and this fluid collected beneath the bone above the meninges, between the brain and the bone; 
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the procedure is as follows if the fluid is between the brain and the bone, and the abscess is small, that you make a wide incision in the middle of the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two nuts, so that the fluid can flow;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the fluid has grown more, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, like this:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the fluid is under the bone, and the signs that you see are the sutures of the head open on each side, and the water spurts out when you press it inside with your hand, and this is not resolved for you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then you must make three incisions in the middle of the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the fluid out.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	Afterwards, bind the incisions with bandages and powders, and apply wine and oil, and leave it like this until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then unbind it, and treat the wound with tents and ointments, and keep the head evenly bandaged, and give the patient dry food with little moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is that you observe or perceive the size of the abscess, and the collection of fluid;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore cut where the abscess appears, and the accumulation of fluid, and split it open as much as you can;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if a flow of blood comes, so that the patient dies from the loss of blood and the evacuation of fluid.
de reume	of rheum/a cold
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone experiences an illness called "catarrh" in the eyes or chest, and the illness is chronic, and medical treatment is not effective, then the last resort is cauterization, along with cutting the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you are about to cut them, that the patient tilt their head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	afterwards rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then have the patient constrict their neck with a cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then observe where the vein pulsates, and the location of each is behind the ears, and a little recessed;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the locations with ink, then cut one and the other with a sharp scalpel in two places, so that the cut reaches the bone, and this should be across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you wish, place the scalpel under the artery and cut it from above, cutting like two fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood spurts upwards continuously.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery cannot be felt, then you must measure the distance of three fingers, then mark with ink and cut to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the necessary amount of blood to let out is six hundred (600 ml), and perhaps a little more or less, depending on what the patient can tolerate, and the fullness of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if any of the periosteum remains on the bone, cut it so that no abscesses form there, then tighten the wound and bind it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes, and acute catarrh, because of the moisture of tears and the heat in the temples and chronic raging headache and similar things, and he is treated with various medical cures and none of it helps him, we should open the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the way to open them is for the patient to pull back the hair from his temples, and pay attention to the artery that appears in the temple, because it is clearly visible by its pulsation, and is rarely hidden except in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is hidden, the patient should tighten his neck with some cloth, then rub the area with some rough cloth, and sprinkle the area with hot water until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula which has this form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then lightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it up with the forceps, and separate it well from the tissues that are underneath it on each side;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, turn it with the point of the hook, then cut it on that side according to the size of the two heads.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood will not spurt out completely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw blood from six hundred up to three hundred;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread, so that no decay comes before the healing of the wound, and bleeding occurs;
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut the excess between the two ties at that very moment, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with the cutting cautery down to the bone until the heads are severed;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and that is the better way, if the patient has no fever and is of a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cautery helps to dry up moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	therefore it is of greater help with moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or it is necessary for the extraction of arteries that one fills the place with old cotton and puts on well-made tents;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are untied, they should be treated with drying medications that promote flesh growth, and with tents, until healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if blood flows from the artery while you are working, hasten to stop it with cautery, or fill the place with vitriol and compress it with your hand until the bleeding is stopped;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you don't have that available, put your finger on the spot until the blood clots, and sprinkle the area with cold water until the bleeding stops, and compress it as needed;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and what is better and easier in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery from two sides, but the cutting edges should be quite thick to retain their heat longer. 
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it holds its heat less.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be a finger's width of space between the two blades, and then when you have marked the two places with ink, and you place the burning iron on it until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they should be spaced apart between the two ends for it is not completely fused with this cautery from one end to the other;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes descend from the veins that are on the top of the head because of heat, and medical treatment is of no benefit, and you see the patient's face redden, and feel a throbbing in the forehead like a tremor;
