et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the swelling is even down to the depths, because the peritoneum/abdominal wall presses upon the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign, when it is from a tear in the peritoneum/abdominal wall, is that it causes sudden pain at the onset, and the swelling appears uneven, close under the skin, and this is because of the protrusion of the intestine and body outside of the peritoneum/abdominal wall.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the omentum descends with the intestine, and is retained there, and causes the patient to suffer great pain, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments, one is afraid of iron (cautery), so it should be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way to do this is to instruct the patient to put the intestine back inside the wound with his hand, if he can put it back in;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then he should be supported on his neck between your hands, and lift his thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then spread the scrotum above, and cut all the skin of the testicles lengthwise;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert hooks into the lips of the incision as needed to open the wound, and they should be such that the egg can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then peel away the tunic which is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white tunic is uncovered on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then put your index finger into that which follows the testicle, into that which is between the white tunic which is under the skin of the egg, and between the second tunic, and separate that which is behind the egg, and between the second tunic;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move with your right hand inside the scrotum, and stretch the white tunic upwards with your left hand, and lift the testicle with all the tunic towards the incision;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to stretch the testicle upwards, and untie that which is attached behind the ligature;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and search with your fingers if there is any of the intestine wrapped in the hard white tunic, and if you find any, push it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a thick thread made of ten strands, and put it in the back part of the tunic, which is behind the skin of the scrotum;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the incision, then cut the ends of the threads that appear, so that there are four threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then bring them together, one on top of the other, in the form of a cross, and tie the tunic, which we said is under the skin of the scrotum, with a strong ligature in two places;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the ends of the threads and tie them tightly in two places, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter it, preventing an abscess from forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place another ligature along the first ligature, two fingers' length from it, and after these two ligatures, leave a finger's width of the tunic, which is under the skin of the scrotum;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then all the rest, following the roundness of the testicle;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is under the skin of the scrotum, until the blood and pus flow, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool soaked in oil, and place it on the wounds, and apply the ligature that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white tunic that we have mentioned is cauterized, after the incision, for fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the ligature until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is slow to fall off, then it should be moistened with warm water, and apply what we have said, until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this affliction, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with a knife.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the hernia that is together with the screw, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above them lightly underneath; 
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut it in the middle, and treat the abscess with something that opens it, until the vessels fall off;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture comes in the groin, as we have said, and the place opens;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines descend into the testicles, and if some do descend, it is little, and returns all the time;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if it remains too long in this state, the wound or fistula grows, until the intestine descends;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens because of the extension of the fistula that is in the groin, as we have said, for it is extended, then the place softens and swells and opens;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and the patient lies supine between your hands, then cut the swollen place of the rupture widely, about the width of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the fistula that is under the skin that follows it, then take the thread and put it on the visible place of the fistula;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it deep into the belly, then sew the two visible places of the fistula over the end of the thread, and sew both;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull the end of the thread, and do not cut the fistula or spread egg or anything else, as I have taught you in the treatment of intestinal hernia;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it by the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean it and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The fistula is constricted, and has no opening in the rupture, and the cautery is more moderate in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often the skin of the testicles is softened in some men, because the flesh inside is softened, and it is milky in appearance;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wants to treat it, to make the patient lie on his back, and cut the skin that is softened down to the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then join the two edges with a suture, and if you wish, first sew the excess of the softened skin with three or four sutures firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cut between the sutures, and treat it like other wounds, until it is healed, and the threads fall out.
dou chastrement	of castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is condemned in our law, and therefore I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is only necessary for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one is that the physician should know how to answer when asked about it, and know the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate some animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by pulling, or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by pulling, we make the animal sit in hot water, until the testicles are softened and hanging down;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand, until they are drawn back and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castration by cutting:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you must restrain the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the spermatic cord, and cut each testicle with one cut, once you have skinned them well;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave there some of the thick and thin membranes which are on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that which is done by pulling, because with pulling, some part of the testicles might remain, by which the animal still desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism exists in two ways in humans:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two testicles appears something like the form of a woman's nature, where there is hair, and sometimes urine flows there.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other type is in women, and they have above the pubis something like a penis and two testicles. 
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for the man and the woman is that you cut away all the added flesh and treat them like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second type, for men whose urine spurts through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	Of tentigo (a skin disease, likely referring to a sexually transmitted infection).
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigo is an extra growth of flesh on the genitals, so much so that it is very ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as big as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must grasp the excess of the tentigo in your hand or with hooks, and cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and there is another growth that arises at the opening of the vagina, and fills it, and sometimes protrudes, and has the appearance of a tail, and therefore the ancients called it "tailed malady".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	So you must cut it, as we have described for the tentigo, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	of erysipelas
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erysipelas occurs when a woman's nature is not pierced, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or accidental through illness that has come there;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is because of added flesh, or from thin or thick syphac, and is made deep within the womb, or on the sides, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and it prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps having menses;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the diagnosis of this is by examination of the vulva.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the blockage is clearly apparent, search for it with your fingers or with a probe.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is from thin syphac, and it is near the two lips, hurry, and round it like this:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two index fingers together, and let the woman be on her back, with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then spread the two lips firmly, until the thin syphac is round, and the blockage is opened;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and soak it in oil, and put it on the place, and let the woman lie at home each day, so that it cannot close up.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphac is hard and thick, you must cut it with a myrtle-leaf shaped spatula.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the blockage is of newborn flesh, then lift it with a hook and cut it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have blood-stopping medicines, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, mixed with egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then insert a large lead tube so the wound cannot close;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and leave it there for a long time, and insert a dry linen tent;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when proud flesh grows in the marrow, it should be cut in this manner, unless it is a cancerous abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For a cancerous abscess that is in the marrow, one should not touch it with iron (a surgical instrument).
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows habitually, and when hemorrhoids are old they become bluish/livid;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have already discussed in the division their characteristics and symptoms, and I will discuss here those that can be treated.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and livid swellings, when they are deep in the marrow, and they are not perceptible to the touch, should not be treated with iron (a surgical instrument).
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, that can be felt, are the ones that can be treated.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	You must then place the woman in a cold room, then grasp the hemorrhoid with tongs, and cut it at its roots, then sprinkle on medicines to stop the bleeding, such as acacia and dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things; 
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then have her put her feet against the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding occurs, have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and vinegar, and make a poultice of it on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping glasses to her back and breasts without scarification;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, and soak it in plantain juice or wild rose juice with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess subsides, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and the one that is called "albathir" is red, and is similar to a rough head, it must be cut like I described for the thelul;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses of the marrow
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the marrow, such as canker and stony abscess and herpes and estiomene and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and several other diseases that I mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that occurs in the marrow, which is not among the abscesses that collect pus;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know the work of iron (cautery), see if the abscess is acute at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not rush to pierce it, but let it mature until the pain subsides;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a seat, and have two small seats where they lean, and support their back and bring their feet together towards the lower part of the leg; 
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let their thighs be spread, and place their arms under their knees, and tie them well with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then suck from him towards the right side, and use the instrument with which one opens the mouth of the bladder (urethra), the form of which comes later;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you use this instrument, you first insert the probe to know the depth of the bladder, so that what enters with the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not injure the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is too large, you must cover the depth of the bladder with cloths, so that the instrument does not hurt them;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he must put the funnel of the instrument on top, and hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and it is made soft by hand, it should be cut at the top, with a milk spatula; 
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is emptied, you must put in the wound tents soaked in rose oil, or in dried green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the tent away from the wound in the depth of the bladder, and put outside, on the bladder and on the scalpel, clean wool soaked in water where mallows have been boiled;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it after two days with a suitable ointment, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes the bladder and the wound are cleaned with a clyster of water and honey, and then with water in which roots of lily and long birthwort have been boiled;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is returned to the bladder, you must avoid cauterizing with iron, but treat it as we have described in the section.
de l’enfantement	on childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	The midwife must first understand the process of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman pushing downwards, and desires to smell aromatic scents:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hurries to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then know that this birth is according to the natural process, and the exit is under its head, and the afterbirth with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, you should press lightly on her belly, so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends headfirst, the afterbirth comes out with it, and the womb is cleansed of its excess fluids by a good cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and the one that comes differently does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes feet first, and the body or the head comes out first, and the hands, or it comes out on its stomach, or sideways, and is sometimes turned on its neck, and in other bad positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	so it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these things, and to beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the positions and how one should help.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes headfirst in a natural way, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, have her sit on a chair, where the women will hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and stimulate her nature with oil or cooked fenugreek, and then the midwife should put between her fingers the small spatula of which here is the form: 
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and tear the afterbirth, and cut with her fingernail until the moisture that is inside runs out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give the woman an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her sneeze using condiments, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	the child will come out immediately.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out, you must gently push them back in little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, place the woman on a seat and raise her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then suddenly drop the seat to the ground, and someone should hold the woman so she doesn't fall during the drop;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot enter and the child dies, cut off the hands with the knife previously mentioned, and extract the child, and reposition it properly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the delivery of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes feet first, you must push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little, until it is straight;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take one of the feet and extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When he jumps up to the thighs, instruct her to take them, and make her sneeze with pepper;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	then he will jump out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it doesn't come out as we have said, then turn it little by little until it is in accordance with its natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it comes out easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come out as we have said, then take marshmallow mucilage, and sesame oil, and dissolved gum, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply it to the woman's genitals inside and outside with this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is softened below, make her a pessary of myrrh, and place it inside her, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and press lightly on her belly, for the child will jump out immediately.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the delivery of the child onto its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this manner, the midwife should put her hands there little by little; 
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then it should be supported by its neck, and its feet hanging down, and it should be lying on a bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold its hands little by little, and then take its hands on its belly, and remove the cushions from beneath, so that it is positioned downwards;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, then take its feet and move them strongly, then move its belly upwards, then push your hands there;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and rock the child gently;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to push until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	regarding the delivery of a child who comes out hand first
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	One must skillfully work to bring the hand back:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot bring it back, then have the woman stand up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her lie down on a bed, and raise her legs firmly;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the lubricating preparation that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, have her sit on a seat, then work on bringing the hand back;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and deliver the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and tell her to push until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	with the child coming out onto its neck, and its hands spread out, and its face turned towards its mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the midwife hold her hand, then turn it little by little, and deliver it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, apply a mixture of marshmallow root and oil to the area, as we have said, then tell her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	And when you have done this, have her sit on a chair, and tell her to push;
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In this same way with the entire afterbirth.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way with the entire afterbirth, cut the afterbirth with your fingernail, until the moisture is drained;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if the child hangs by its face and neck, cut it from the navel so that it is not held back and the child dies;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then push the child inside, until you have positioned it as it should be, and tell the woman to bear down sometimes:
adonques si istra legierement.	Then it will come out easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the delivery of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are a strange thing, and do not usually live, except rarely;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know this, that they are multiplied, and are separated by the membrane that divides them, which is attached to the uterus;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they emerge as naturally as a single child, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out with difficulty, treat them as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and do what she does quickly and lightly;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and act in such a way as is best for their well-being.
de plusors enfans	of multiple children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes one or two or three or four or five or six or seven are formed in the womb, or more, up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child by the measure of the glorious wise [God?], and the midwife must know all this, for perhaps such a thing will happen to her;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	so let her act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman with a dead child in the womb, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are compelled to work by hand;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must know if the woman is of sound health, and has no condition where she is afraid of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman should be lying on her back, with her head inclined downwards and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the assistant should hold her from both sides, or she should be tied to the bed so that she is not pulled down with the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the vulva of the mother with moist oils with mucilage of marshmallow and fenugreek and linseed, then have the midwife anoint her hands with these oils and mucilages;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then insert them gently into the vulva, then find a place where she inserts the hooks that are suitable for this, and take care if the child is positioned to descend head first;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	insert the hooks into its eyes or its neck or its mouth or its palate or under the chin or in the fontanelle or near the temples, and if the descent is feet first, insert them in the heel and in the middle of the sides;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he should hold the hook in his right hand, and place the curvature between the fingers of his left hand, and insert it with his whole hand gently, and insert the hook in any of these places that we have mentioned, until it comes to the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the hook:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another hook opposite it, or a third if you need it, so that the extraction is even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then pull it evenly, moving from one side to the other, to cause it to come out, and the hook should be toothed to hold it, as is the shape here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part of it remains, then let the surgeon anoint some of his fingers with oil, and insert them into that part, and pull out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any of it still remains, then place this hook in a higher place, and do this until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot pull it back due to the tightness, then you must wrap a cloth around it, until it comes all the way out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then cut it at the joint of the sole or at the heel, and so you must do with the other hand, and with both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and the birth canal is narrow, or if there is a pointed gathering on the head, you must place the pointed spatula between your fingers, and split the head and extract the fluid;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you break it with the instrument called "almidach", whose form comes with the instruments in the chapter which is after this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and do the same if the child has a naturally large head;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull out the bones with the forceps, and if the head jumps out and is caught in the vulva, let it be split, so that the fluid that is in the worst place comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it in pieces as best you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the fluid flows.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, the extraction is easy, and the straightening at the opening of the womb is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is narrow in the belly or the chest, you must extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut the belly or the chest so the fluid within can flow out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if the other limbs are removed, and the head remains, then the midwife should put her hand deep into the womb and pull it down to the opening of the womb;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then insert one or two hooks, and pull it out forcefully; 
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the opening of the womb is constricted because of a hot abscess that has developed there, do not work on it, but rather administer moist and oily things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply poultices, and sitz baths with softening and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can straighten it, apply what we have said for a live child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then pull it out piece by piece, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply what we have said for hot abscesses that occur in the womb;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, she should be placed in astringent water, and administer other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb a child had died, then another was conceived over that one, and the second also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she developed an abscess in the buttock, and it swelled until it opened, and began to suppurate heavily.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called for the treatment, and I considered it for a long time, and the wound would not heal.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster of strong attraction, and a bone came out, and after a few days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised, because there are no bones in the belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	So I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I searched the wound, and drew out many bones, until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived a long time like this, and a little bit of pus always came out of the place;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I would not have recalled this chapter except for the fact that, when the physician encounters a strange case, he should know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	of returning the marrow to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the shape of the press, with which one squeezes books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and with two turns at the two ends of the two cords.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horn should be more slender than the restrictor, and be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the wood should be one finger wide, and the edge of the boards one finger, and the length a palm and a half;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the middle of the two planks should be two additions of this same wood, which should be attached to each, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two additions are placed at the mouth of the hammer to open it when one turns the two cords.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, resembling it but more slender and lighter, is made of ebony or boxwood, like tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has at the two ends two additions, as you see, of a palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you want to open the hammer with the whole instrument, have the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging and legs open, then put the two additions joined together into the hammer, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then open your hand with the whole instrument, as you did with the tongs evenly, according to how much you want to open the mouth of the hammer, until the midwife does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all surmounted, and their forms are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the physician has prepared them, the work is more rapid, and better for men because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	So do not despise the instrument so that you don't have it prepared, because their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze with pepper, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose; 
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if it comes out because of this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take a pot, and make a hole in the lid, and put in herbs that can open the womb's opening, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, birthwort and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in a pot in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put one end of a tube in the hole of the pot, and the other end in the opening of the womb, and hold it there so that the steam enters the womb;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The afterbirth will come out quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment, and does not come out, then instruct the midwife to wet her left hand in sesame oil or in marshmallow mucilage, and then put it in the vagina, and search for the afterbirth;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, she should take it and pull it little by little, straight out, so that the womb does not fall out during the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but she should move it gently to the right and to the left, and then pull;
si venra et se desaerdra.	thus it will come and be detached.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the womb is already narrowed, we have described the treatment of sneezing, and of fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not come out with all that we have said, be careful not to be foolish in pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but what is at the opening of the womb, you must tie it to the woman's thigh, then administer an enema of tetrapharmacum ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	thus it will rot and soften, and come out;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	however, when it rots, a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So then suitable fumigations are necessary for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients tried fumigation of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for the retention of the flowers and the afterbirth is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass, similar to a cane, and one puts the narrow end in the genitals, and the wide end over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the coals, and let it burn until it is used up, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the anus/rectum
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have a pierced anus, but it is blocked by a thin membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	therefore the midwife must pierce this membrane with her finger, and not pierce it with a sharp spatula, and take care that she does not touch the band (frenulum);
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply wool soaked in wine and oil, then treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you are worried that it will close up again, put a lead tube in the hole, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child needs to go to the toilet.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this blockage comes from the healing of a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	so it is necessary to cut this adhesion:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	then it should be treated, as we have said, with the lead tube.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from below the anus are swellings, and growths that come near the outside of the anus, or in the space between the two parts, and it can be a single fistula or several;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when this swelling is old, it opens and emits moist white pus or thin excrement, and sometimes these fistulas are perforating;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are recognized because there comes out either excrement or flatulence when the patient defecates, and sometimes a worm comes out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to the middle of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and extend up to the hip joint, and up to the base of the spine.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes the fistula penetrating the anus, and the non-penetrating one: 
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you put your index finger in the anus, and insert a thin needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is tortuosity, then insert a thin lead probe, or a horsehair, until you feel the probe or the hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you don't feel it, and no discharge or flatulence or worms come from the opening, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not penetrate;
si te haste dou curer.	so hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula penetrates to the bladder or to the urethra, urine will leak out, and it cannot be healed with medicines. 
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced to the hip joint, then the probe reaches that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no tortuosity and the source of the pain is around it, then pus constantly comes out, and neither medicine nor healing ointment is effective;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these penetrating fistulas there is no cure but work, and the vanity of foolish physicians who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In one that is not penetrating and is not old, there is hope of healing by surgery, as I have experienced, and the patient should lie on their back in your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and lift their legs up to their thighs, and have their thighs bent towards their belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a probe of brass, or of lead if there is tortuosity, until you know where the probe reaches.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, then you should insert your index finger there, then feel if the probe has pierced it;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and if it is uncovered where you feel between your finger the abdominal wall or the flesh, then you know that it is penetrating;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	so do not work on it because it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said, however, that some can be healed, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help that is given is to heat the thin cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and insert it, very hot, into the fistula, until it reaches near the rectum;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that these decayed tissues are burned, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with tents soaked in butter, until this tissue comes out, then treat it with ointment that generates flesh and heals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If not, it cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the probe enters, and does not reach down to the finger that is in the rectum, and between your finger and the probe there is a thick covering of flesh or tissue, and you see the fistula below that which follows the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	then cut it from the beginning of the fistula, and push the probe further in, and then the cautery after it, until it reaches the end of the probe;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the probe will be released, and will fall out;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then clean the damaged tissues that resemble a bird's feather, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood overcomes you, and flows between you and the work, cauterize it with fire or a sharp medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of this excess flesh, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat it with tents soaked in butter or in crushed things, until the place produces pus, and the burnt flesh comes out with the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with generating, drying ointments that produce hard flesh, and these are dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula reaches deep into the anus, and is far from the body, put your finger into the anus and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between the two is the cloth or the syfac or flesh, or it is close to piercing through, then there is nothing but a path of confidence and hope, by the application of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it all the way to the bottom, or if you can, you insert tents and treat it as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so that you do not cut the tissue that holds the anus, and the excrement comes out involuntarily;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut near the anus, either with a tent or another suitable instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then clean the damaged flesh that is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then work to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula in the area outside the anus:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	thus it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes there are fistulas in this way:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is in the side of the anus near the skin above, then take a tent pierced at the end in this way:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And put a twisted thread doubled, and put the tent with the thread into the fistula until it is at the end.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces the edge of the anus inside, then pull the thread out of that hole, so that you put your finger in the anus;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the end of the thread, and bring the two ends together, and tie one to the other, and leave it for a day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and tighten it sometimes, until the thread cuts the flesh that is between the two, and they fall off;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is closed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce, make it pierce in any way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not necessary to cut too deeply for the ligature, and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the pointed scalpel with which one cuts the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and not on the other, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids are of two kinds:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	either they are inside the anus, like a grain of resin, and there are small and large ones, and blood constantly flows from them, and there is one or more, and they are outside the anus and at the end of the anus;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are outside have little moisture, and constantly leak a little yellow water or a little blood, and have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain while going to the toilet, so that the anus protrudes, and the threads appear;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	then hurry, and grasp it with forceps, or hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the hooks cannot hold them because of their moisture, grasp them with a cloth, or with cotton, or with a piece of chamois;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and powder over them some hot powders that act as a cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as described in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the rectum cannot protrude, give the patient a biting and harsh enema to cleanse what is in the rectum, so that it can come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When the patient strains, and if the threads are far from the anus, then the treatment is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you take them with your fingernail or with tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until healed, and so they avoid the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You must administer the suture in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take a twisted thread, and put it in a needle, and then pull the thread over and make the needle pierce the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and it should be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread firmly, then knot the thread, and pull out the needle, and do this with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then put on the wound a cloth moistened with rose oil or cerate, and put it on the wound, and tell the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, then treat them with ointment and other treatments, until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of the drying of the excrement or anus/rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times drying of the excrement occurs in the intestine, and by constriction of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	So you must scrape the bark from the surface with the tip of a spatula or your fingernail, which prevents it from moistening;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is consolidated as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot consolidate, then repeat the scraping more forcefully than before, until it heals well, and is excoriated/raw;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	of ash tree
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Formice is a small, misshapen/irregular appearance around the body, and it goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the cold finds it, and it feels as if numb with cold, and it occurs all over the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere. 
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place this quill upon the formice, so that the circle encompasses the formice all around;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand with the quill until you cut all around the formice, and put it in deep, and pull out the formice by its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a quill made of brass or iron according to this shape, and it should be thin underneath and sharp on top:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	not sharp enough to pierce, so that it can be held by the finger, and also pressed.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the formice, as described earlier in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a clyster is made of silver, or tin, or cast or hammered brass;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these instruments are made small and large, depending on to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those then which are administered in the treatment of children, and who are weak and suffering, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the clyster, small and large, is wider at the top, where the belly is tied, in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be a separation where the belly is tied, as you see, and the bottom should be pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and it has two holes on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly, where the medicines are put, should be made of an animal bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes, and there should be a finger's width between each hole, then put a strong thread of raw flax, twisted tenfold or around it into these holes, and gather the belly like a goat's udder;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument at the front with a strong thread, then administer the clyster;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And the medicine should be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the tip of the clyster with oil or egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the practitioner squeezes it with both hands together, until it is completely empty, then withdraws the clyster, and the patient raises their legs against the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, they hold it in as long as they can;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if they sleep a whole night with it, it is even more helpful.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you give a clyster for diarrhea, and the medicine comes out quickly, repeat it until they are healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if there are hemorrhoids in the anus, or an abscess, the clyster should be as thin as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the thin clyster for when the leather is tight:
des plaies	of wounds/from wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken in the division about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	now we will tell you the treatments by hand and by medicine, according to completion.
